<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйственный.html>хозя́йственный</a> (4091)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйство.html>хозя́йство</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xozjájstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-енный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйственный.html>хозя́йственный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xozjájstvennyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)хозя́йственнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)хозя́йственней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>economic <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">relating to the economy</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйственный.html>хозя́йственная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деятельность.html>де́ятельность</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xozjájstvennaja</b> déjatelʹnostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">economic activity</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> household
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйственный.html>хозя́йственный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:магазин.html>магази́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xozjájstvennyj</b> magazín</i> ― <span class="e-translation">household shop</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>thrifty, economical</li>
<li>practical <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">having skills or knowledge that are practical</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***хозяйство.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйство.html>хозяйство</a> (1577)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяин.html>хозя́ин</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xozjáin</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйство.html>хозя́йство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xozjájstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйство.html>хозя́йства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйство.html>хозя́йства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйство.html>хозя́йств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>economy</li>
<li>household, household effects, household articles, stuff, things</li>
<li>enterprise, farm</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">euphemistic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> manhood, package (male genitalia)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйство.html>хозя́йство</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xozjájstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***хоккей.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хоккей.html>хокке́й</a> (11803)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hockey</i>.
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холить.html>хо́лить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xólitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-еный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-enyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>
<ol><li>well-groomed</li>
<li><i>This term needs a translation to English. Please help out and <b>add a translation</b>, then remove the text <code> |  | rfdef |  | </code>.</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Short forms <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холеный.html>хо́лен</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:холеный.html>хо́лена</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:холеный.html>хо́лено</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:холеный.html>хо́лены</a></span> theoretically exist, but are usually avoided due to their similarity to short forms of the past passive participle of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холить.html>хо́лить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xólitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cherish, to groom</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:холестерин.html>холестери́н</a> (25634)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холестерин.html>холестери́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xolesterín, xolestɛrín</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холестерин.html>холестери́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холестерин.html>холестери́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холестерин.html>холестери́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cholesterol (an essential component of mammalian cell membranes)</li></ol>

<p>Per Vasmer, probably derived from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хохол.html>хохо́л</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xoxól</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crest</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:холл.html>холл</a> (4376)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hall</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холл.html>холл</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xoll</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холл.html>хо́лла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холл.html>хо́ллы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холл.html>хо́ллов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lobby, foyer, hall</li>
<li>large vestibule</li></ol>

***холм.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:холм.html>холм</a> (2001)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xъlmъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холм.html>холм</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xolm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холм.html>холма́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холм.html>холмы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холм.html>холмо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hill
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1868</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Leo_Tolstoy" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Leo Tolstoy">Leo Tolstoy</a>,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:война.html>Война́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>мир</a></cite>  | <cite>War and Peace</cite> | , <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>том</a> I, <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>часть</a> III, <a href = vnd.unilang:глава.html>глава́</a> XV:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впереди.html>впереди́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:далеко.html>далеко́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:берег.html>берегу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:туманный.html>тума́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>мо́ря</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:виднеться.html>видне́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выступающий.html>выступа́ющие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лесистый.html>леси́стые</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:холм.html>холмы́</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:должный.html>должна́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>была́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприятельский.html>неприя́тельская</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:армия.html>а́рмия</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:виднеться.html>видне́лось</a> что́-то.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vperedí, dalekó, na tóm beregú tumánnovo mórja, vidnélisʹ vystupájuščije lesístyje <b>xolmý</b>, na kotóryx dolžná bylá bytʹ neprijátelʹskaja ármija, i vidnélosʹ štó-to.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">In front, far off on the farther shore of that sea of mist, some wooded <b>hills</b> were discernible, and it was there the enemy probably was, for something could be descried.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Accent pattern <i>a</i> (<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холм.html>хо́лма</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:холм.html>хо́лмы</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:холм.html>хо́лмах</a></span>, etc.) is found in Church Slavonic<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> and classical poetry, e.g. in Pushkin:
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1829</b>,  Alexander Pushkin,  “На <a href = vnd.unilang:холм.html>холмах</a> Грузии  | On the Hills of Georgia | ”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:северный.html>Се́верные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цветы</a></cite>  | <cite>Northern Flowers</cite> | , published 1831:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:холм.html>хо́лмах</a></b> гру́зии <a href = vnd.unilang:лежать.html>лежи́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночной.html>ночна́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мгла.html>мгла́</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na <b>xólmax</b> Grúzii ležít nočnája mglá.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">On the hills of Georgia lies a nightly darkness.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></dd></dl>

***холод.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:холод.html>хо́лод</a> (1705)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xoldъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">coolness, cold</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хлад</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xlad</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холод.html>хо́лод</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xólod</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холод.html>хо́лода</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холод.html>холода́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холод.html>холодо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cold <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">low temperature</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холодевший.html>холоде́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xolodévšij</span>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холод.html>хо́лод</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xólod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холодеть.html>холоде́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xolodétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похолодеть.html>похолоде́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grow cold
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:холодеть.html>холоде́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ужас.html>у́жаса</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xolodétʹ</b> ot úžasa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to grow cold with terror</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холод.html>хо́лод</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xólod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холодить.html>холоди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xolodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cool, to make cold</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> also  impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cause a feeling of coolness
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мятый.html>мя́та</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:холодить.html>холоди́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рот.html>рту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mjáta <b>xolodít</b> vo rtu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">mint cools the mouth</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мятый.html>мя́ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:холодить.html>холоди́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рот.html>рту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ot mjáty <b>xolodít</b> vo rtu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">mint cools the mouth</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холодный.html>холо́дный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xolódnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холодный.html>хо́лодно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xólodno</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-хо́лодно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)холодне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-хо́лодно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)холодне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>coldly</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Predicative">Predicative</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холодный.html>хо́лодно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xólodno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>one is cold
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:холодный.html>хо́лодно</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne <b>xólodno</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'm <b>cold</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холодный.html>хо́лодно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xólodno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холодный.html>холо́дный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xolódnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***холодный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:холодный.html>холо́дный</a> (661)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xoldьnъ</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хла́дный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xládnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic. Synchronically analysable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холод.html>хо́лод</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xólod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холодный.html>холо́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xolódnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)холодне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)холодне́й</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">холодне́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cold</li></ol>

***холоп.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:холоп.html>холо́п</a> (17071)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xolpъ</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">хлапъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xlapŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with the same meaning or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">chłop</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">peasant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холоп.html>холо́п</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xolóp</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холоп.html>холо́па</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холоп.html>холо́пы</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холоп.html>холо́пья</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холоп.html>холо́пи</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холоп.html>холо́пов</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холоп.html>холо́пьев</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холоп.html>холо́пей</a><sup>*</sup></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Both irregular plurals are archaic.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> serf, bondman, kholop</li></ol>

***холостой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:холостой.html>холосто́й</a> (11442)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xolstъ(jь)</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">хластъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xlastŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">hlȃst</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:холостой.html>хо́лост</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xólost</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холостой.html>холосто́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xolostój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)холосте́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)холосте́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>single <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">not married</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>idle <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">not working</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> idle, free-running
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:холостой.html>холосто́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>ход</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xolostój</b> xod</i> ― <span class="e-translation">idling</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ballistics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> blank</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Per Zaliznyak, the comparative <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">холосте́е</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xolostéje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is rare and awkward.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холостой.html>холосто́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xolostój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холостой.html>холосто́го</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холостой.html>холосты́е</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холостой.html>холосты́х</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холостой.html>холоста́я</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>unmarried person, single person, bachelor</li>
<li>blank <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">bullet</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***холостяк.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:холостяк.html>холостя́к</a> (13158)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холостой.html>холосто́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xolostój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>двум</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоявший.html>стоя́вшим</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сарай.html>сара́ем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сани.html>саня́м</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nikíta v éto vrémja užé nadél <b>xomút</b>, podvjazál sedjólku, obítuju gvózdikami, i, v  odnój ruké nesjá ljóxkuju krášenuju dugú, a v drugój vedjá lóšadʹ, podxodíl k dvum stojávšim pod sarájem sanjám</i></dd><dd>meanwhile Nikita put the <b>horse collar</b>, tied the saddle studded with nails and -carrying a worn-out shaft bow on one hand and leading the horse with the other- approached towards two sleighs which lay under the shed</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> yoke, clamp</li></ol>
